Y%S ,xld m%cd;dka;%sl iudcjd§ ckrcfha .eiÜ m;%h
The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka
(Published by Authority)
PART IV (B) — LOcAL  GOVERNmENT
Local Government Notification
1a- pG 5972 - 07 (09/2022) 
This Gazette Extraordinary can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
Pradeshiya sabha rideegama
It is hereby notified for public information that it has been adopted under resolution No. 5/1  moved at the General Confer-
ence held on 18.08.2022  at Pradeshiya Sabha Rideegama that all the roads and thoroughfares for which legal action had not 
been filed in a proper  Judicial Court before the date specified  or roads and thoroughfares confirmed as the roads and thor-
oughfares that should be owned by Pradeshiya Sabha Rideegama  as per the Decree of a Judicial Court in which a case had 
been filed before the said date and not mentioned in the following schedule from among the roads and thoroughfares given 
in the list of the schedule of the notification published in the Extraordinary Gazette No. 2277/36  and dated 27.04.2022  and 
Amendment Extraordinary Gazette No. 2287/15 dated 05.07.2022, shall be confirmed as roads and thoroughfares owned by 
the Pradeshiya Sabha Rideegama in terms of orders made by the series of “ Orders on publication of notifications specifying 
preparation of plans and lists for roads and thoroughfares maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabha within the North Western 
Province” published by Extraordinary  Gazette No. 2238/35 and dated 30
th  July 2021 by the Hon. Governor in the North 
Western Province and in terms of the Order by Section 24(1) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 0f 1987.
It is further notified that a list of said roads and thoroughfares has been included in the schedule hereto and all the  
roads and thoroughfares mentioned in that schedule shall be considered as roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya 
Sabha Rideegama under Sub-Section (5) of Section 24 of Pradeshiya Sabha Act. 
 
 
K.Wilbert Kulathunga,
 Chairman, 
 Pradeshiya Sabha Rideegama. 
16th September 2022,
At the Head Office, Pradeshiya  Sabha Rideegama.

Pradeshiya Sabha Rideegama Proposes that the roads and thoroughfares for which legal actions had not been filed in a proper Judicial  Court and not mentioned in 
the following schedule from among the roads and thoroughfares given in the list of the schedule of the notification published in the Gazette No. 2277/36  and dated 
27.04.2022  and Amendment Extraordinary Gazette No. 2287/15 dated 05.07.2022, according to the resolution No. 5/1 made at the Pradeshiya Sabha Conference 
held on 18.08.2022, shall be confirmed as roads and thoroughfares owned by the Pradeshiya Sabha Rideegama in terms of orders made by the series of “ Orders 
on publication of notifications specifying preparation of plans and lists for roads and thoroughfares maintained by the Pradeshiya Sabha within the North Western 
Province” published by Extraordinary Gazette No. 2238/35 and dated 30
th  July 2021 by the Hon. Governor in the North Western Province and in terms of the 
Order by Section 24(1) of Pradeshiya Sabha Act, No. 15 0f 1987.
